Nowadays , public transport has become a more topic .
The way of leaving public transportation aside is widely supported in developed countries , but this idea is rejected in developing countries , like the time I live in .
As a matter of fact , car leadership have increased over the last decades reducing the anoint of people using public transport .
The possibility of travelling in their own cars is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or even worse , the use of waiting time in a long queues .
Nevertheless , you have another side to this beauty .
There are people who can not afford to have their own cars or maybe they can afford to travel by any other means of transportation than the one provided by the local government .
There are countries where bus is so expensive that people choose to pay the bus best rather than paying for a full car .
Similarly , people in countries with less incoke turn to these services because it is a way to reduce their overall expenses .
To conclude , the future of public transport will depend on the way people gtove it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , and in others where they will need it as long as their economy needs it .
People need easy , fast and cheap solutions .
In general , using a car is easier then taking a train or a bus .
It 's just eart your house or your office .
You do n't have to go to a station by walking , catryinf weights , or suffering because of the train or the snoe .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply you do n't like to drive , you can find easier to take a public transport .
And all more enjoyable : you can relax running to the music and looking around , or reading newspapers and books .
Is the car faster the public transport ?
It depends .
The traffic can affect cars and buses at the same level .
Sometimes cars are faster then buses , sometimes buses are faster .
Speed trains are always faster than cars .
Speaking about money ? Travelling by car seems cheaper than public transport .
But , if we consider all the expenses ( buying the car , paying the insurance , etc . ) , maybe cars are not so cheap .
In fact , in every awspwct there are pros and cons .
What about the environment and the quality of life in the cities ?
Public transport is absolutely better .
So , even if travelling by car can be more convenient at a metro level , public transport has to be performed by good citizens and properly sipportec by governments .

Global warming and its consequences in 2015
The Gjarduan 's article " World 's climate about to enter ' uncharted territory ' as it passes 1C of warming " , published on the 9rh Nhovelber 2015 , describes the problems of global warming .
Referring to scientists at the Britsh Met Office , 2015 is going to be the year when the milestone of 1C warming will be broken - dahsed by global warming - which will lead to unonown consequences on the future .
The World Meteorolovicaql Organization made known publicly that 2015 has been the hottest year on record as well as it has cause more carbon dioxide on average by bufnnig fossil fyels .
These problems just announced recently will be issues to talk about at the UN summit in Paris in three weeks .

The Future of Public transport
When we imagine future , we frequently imagine ovecrrowded use and daily subway trains .
As technologies develop and become cheaper more and more people buy personal cars .
A car allows us to move faster and not to depend on others .
Travelling by car is also much more convenient .
Does this all mean that the years of public transportation come to an end ?
In my opinion , it is not true .
Firstly , there will always the people who will not be able to afford to buy a car .
Students , children for large families , old people will continue to use public transportation for a long time .
Secondly , cars can also known into public transport .
Science fiction often deserves future as the world where cars are used freely .
none can use the nearest car he or her use .
Thirdly , people do not have an inborn driving skill , so even in the future children and teenagers will need public transportation .
This is also true for older people , who lose the ability to drive as they age .
In conclusion , public transportation is not likely to dksappeqr , at least during the next tens of years .
